			NOT = { country_exists = CRY }

		}

		eqs_not_has_civil_war = yes
		CRY = { 
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT

			}
		}
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = eqs_support_harmony
	}
	allow_branch = {
		NOT = { is_EQS_SOL = yes }
	}
	relative_position_id = eqs_support_harmony
	x = -3
	y = 1
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus increase_presense_inCRY"

			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
				CRY = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			add_political_power = 100
			CRY = { add_autonomy_ratio = { value = -0.03 } }
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = 100
			CRY = { add_stability = 0.09 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_historical_focus_on = no CRY = { is_ai = yes } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = increase_presense_inCRY_tt
		}
	}
	search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
}
